#include <vector>
#include <iostream>
#include <algorithm>
using namespace std;


int main() {
    long trucks,source,dest,price;
    cin  >> trucks >> source >> dest >> price;
    vector<long> path1,path2;
    long temp;
    if(source==dest)
    {
        cout << trucks*price;
        return 0;
    }
    temp = source;
    while(temp){
        path1.push_back(temp);
        temp = temp/2;
    }
    temp = dest;
    while(temp){
        path2.push_back(temp);
        temp  = temp/2;
    }
    long len1 = path1.size();
    long len2 = path2.size();
    long find=0;
    long flag=0;
    for(long i=0 ; i<len1 ; i++){
        for(long j=0 ; j<len2 ; j++){
            if(path1[i]==path2[j]){
                find = path1[i];
                flag=1;
                break;
            }
        }
            if(flag==1)
                break;
        }
        long cost1=0,cost2=0,cost=0;
         cost1 = trucks*price;
        
         temp = source;
        while(temp!=find){
            cost2 = cost2 + trucks*abs(temp - temp/2) + temp/2;
            temp = temp/2;
        }
         temp = dest;
         while(temp!=find){
            cost2= cost2 + trucks*abs(temp - temp/2)+temp/2;
             temp = temp/2;
        }
        cost2 = cost2-find;
        cost= cost1-cost2;
        cout << cost;
        
       return 0; 
        
    }

using namespace std;

int main(){
    long t;
    cin >> t;
   for(long i=0 ; i<t ; i++){
    long n,e;
    long src;
    cin >> n >> e;
    vector<long> adj[n+1];
    for(long i=0 ; i<e ; i++){
        long a,b;
        cin >> a >> b;
        adj[a].push_back(b);
        adj[b].push_back(a);
    }
    cin >> src;
    
    long dist[n+1];
    for(long i=1 ; i<=n ; i++) dist[i] = 200000;
    queue<long> q;
    dist[src] = 0;
    q.push(src);
    while(q.empty()==false){
        long node = q.front();
        q.pop();
        for(auto it:adj[node]){
            if(dist[node] + 1<dist[it]){
                dist[it]=dist[node]+1;
                q.push(it);
            }
        }
    }
    long idx=0,max=0;
    for(long i=1 ; i<=n ; i++){
        if(dist[i] >= max && dist[i]!=200000){
            max = dist[i];
            idx = i;
        }
    }
    cout << max*2+1 <<" "<< idx <<"\n";
    }
    return 0;
}

16/10/22, 16:58 - GauraV: x = list(map(int,input().rstrip().split(" ")))
memoryElements = list(map(int,input().rstrip().split(" ")))

size = x[0]
windowSize = x[1]

s = sum(memoryElements)
i = 0
index = 0
freeMemory = 0
for j in range(4):
    x=True
    for i in range(size-windowSize+1):
        if x:
            temp = sum(memoryElements[i:i+windowSize])
            x = False
        else:
            temp = temp - memoryElements[i-1] + memoryElements[windowSize+i-1] 
        if temp>freeMemory:
            freeMemory = temp
            index = i
    print(f"{s-freeMemory} {freeMemory}")
    memoryElements = memoryElements[:index] + [freeMemory] + memoryElements[index+windowSize:]
    size = index + windowSize+1
    i = index - windowSize -1

  int fuel,vendors;
    cin >> fuel >> vendors;
    vector<int> vend(vendors,0);
    vector<int> cost(vendors,0);
    for(int i=0 ; i<vendors ; i++){
        cin >> vend[i];
    }
    for(int i=0 ; i<vendors ; i++){
        cin >> cost[i];
    }
   
    int price=0;
    while(fuel){
        int min=100000000;
        int ind=0;
        for(int i=0 ; i<vendors ; i++){
            if(( cost[i] < min) && vend[i]!= 0){
                min = cost[i];
                ind = i;
            }
        }
        
            if((fuel - vend[ind])>=0){
                fuel = fuel-vend[ind];
                price = price + cost[ind]*vend[ind];
            }
            else{
                price = price + cost[ind]*fuel;
                fuel=0;
            }
        vend[ind] = 0;
        }
    
    cout << price;
    return 0;
}

using namespace std;

typedef struct node {
    int val;
    struct node* left;
    struct node* right;
}node;

void find(node* root, int src, vector<int> &path){
    while(root->val!=src){
        if(root->val == src){
            path.push_back(src);
            return;
        }
    
    if(root->val > src){
        path.push_back(root->val);
        root = root->left;
    }
    else{
        path.push_back(root->val);
        root = root->right;
        }
    }
    path.push_back(src);
}


// void print(node* root){
//         if(root  == nullptr){
//             return;
//         }
//         print(root->left);
//         cout << root->val <<" " ; 
//         print(root->right);
// }
node* lowestCommonAncestor(node* root, int p, int q){
    if(root==NULL || root->val == p || root->val == q)
            return root;
        node* left = lowestCommonAncestor(root->left,p,q);
        node* right = lowestCommonAncestor(root->right,p,q);
        if(left==NULL)
            return right;
        else if(right==NULL)
            return left;
        else
            return root;
 }


int main(){

    // #ifndef a
    // freopen("input.txt","r",stdin);
    // freopen("output.txt","w",stdout);
    // #endif
    node* root = nullptr;
    int n ; cin >> n; int src, dest; cin >> src >> dest;
    bool flag;
    for(int i=0 ; i<n ; i++){
        int val ; cin >> val;
        if(root == nullptr){
            root = new node();
            root->val = val;
        }
        else{
            node* temp = root;
            flag = true;
            while(flag){
                if(val > temp->val){
                    if(temp->right){
                        temp = temp->right;
                        continue;
                    }
                    else{
                        node* newnode = new node();
                        newnode->val = val;
                        temp->right = newnode;
                        flag = false;
                    }
                }
                else
                {
                        if(temp->left){
                            temp = temp->left;
                            continue;
                        }
                        else{
                            node* newnode = new node();
                            newnode->val = val;
                            temp->left = newnode;
                            flag = false;

                        }
                    
                }
            }
        }

    }
  node* temp =  lowestCommonAncestor(root,src,dest);
    int count=0;
    vector<int> path;
    find(temp,src,path);
     reverse(path.begin(),path.end());
    find(temp,dest,path);
    
    // cout << temp->val;
   
    // for(int i=0 ; i<path.size() ; i++){
    //     cout << path[i] <<" ";
    // }
    
    // print(root);
    int c=0;
    int f = 0;
    for(int i=0 ; i<path.size()-1 ; i++){
        if(path[i] > path[i+1]){
            if(f!=1 ){
                c++;
                f=1;
            }
        }
        else if(path[i] < path[i+1]){
            if(f!=2){
                f =2;
                c++;
            }
        }
    }
    if(root->val == src || root->val == dest)
        c = c-1;
    
    cout << c <<" " <<path.size()-2;
}

        if(flag){
        for(int i=0 ; i<m ; i++){
            sum = sum + call[i];
            flag = false;
            
        }
        }
        else{
            sum = sum - call[i-1] + call[i+m-1];
        }
        
       if( sum > max){
           max = sum;
           ind = i;
       }
    }
       
        long count=0;
    call.erase(call.begin() + ind, call.begin() + ind  + m -1);
        n = n-2;
        
        
        cout << res-max <<" "<< max <<"\n";
        call[ind]=max;
       
       x--;
}
    return 0;
}

16/11/22, 11:06 - Aditya Shrivastava Bits: #include <cmath>
#include <cstdio>
#include <vector>
#include <iostream>
#include <algorithm>
#include <climits>
using namespace std;

void subSum(vector<int> q, int n) {
    int ans = INT_MIN;
    int curr = 0;
    
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        curr = max(curr+q[i], q[i]);
        ans = max(ans, curr);
    }
    
    cout << ans << " ";
}

void seqSum(vector<int> q, int n) {
    sort(q.begin(), q.end());
    int ans = 0;
    
    int i;
    for (i = n-1; i>= 0; i--){
        if (q[i] < 0) {
            break;
        }
        ans += q[i];
    }
    
    if (ans == 0) {
        if (i >= 0) {
            ans = q[i];
        }
    }
    
    cout << ans << " ";
}

void subLen(vector<int> q, int n) {
    int ans = INT_MIN;
    int temp = 1;
    
    int lo = 0;
    int hi = 1;
    
    while (hi < n) {
        if (q[hi] > q[hi-1]) {
            temp++;
            hi++;
        } else {
            ans = max(ans, temp);
            temp = 1;
            lo = hi;
            hi = lo+1;
        }
    }
    
    ans = max(ans, temp);
    
    cout << ans << " ";
}

int seqLen(vector<int> q, int n) {
    vector<int> res;
    for(int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        auto it = std::lower_bound(res.begin(), res.end(), q[i]);
        if(it==res.end()) res.push_back(q[i]);
        else *it = q[i];
    }
    
    return res.size();
}

int main() {
    int t;
    cin >> t;
    
    while (t--) {
        int n;
        cin >> n;
        vector<int> q(n);
        
        for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
            cin >> q[i];
        }
        
        subSum(q, n);
        seqSum(q, n);
        subLen(q, n);
        cout << seqLen(q, n) << " ";
        cout << endl;
    }
    
    return 0;
}

18/11/22, 00:49 - GauraV: #include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;


int main(){

    // #ifndef ONLINE_JUDGEB
    // freopen("input.txt","r",stdin);
    // freopen("output.txt","w",stdout); 
    // #endif

    long N, e, cost; cin >> N >> e >> cost;
    vector<pair<long,long>>  adj[N+1];
    
    long a, b, wt;
    for(long i=0 ; i<e ; i++){
        cin >> a >> b >> wt;
        adj[a].push_back(make_pair(b,wt));
        adj[b].push_back(make_pair(a,wt));
    }

    long parent[N+1];

    long key[N+1] ;

    bool mstset[N+1];

    for(long i=1 ; i<=N ; i++){
        key[i] = INT_MIN;
         mstset[i] = false;
         parent[i] = -1;
    }

    priority_queue<pair<long, long> > pq;
    key[1] = 0;
    parent[1] = -1;
    pq.push({0,1});
    for(long count=0 ; count < e ; count++){
        long u = pq.top().second;
        pq.pop();
        mstset[u] = true;


        for(auto it : adj[u]){
            long v = it.first;
            long weight = it.second;
            if(mstset[v] == false && weight > key[v]){
                key[v] = weight;
                pq.push({key[v],v});
                parent[v] = u;
                
            }
        }
        
    }
    long sum=0;
    for(long i=1 ; i<=N; i++)
        sum+=key[i];
    
cout << sum*cost;
    
    return 0;
    
}

#include <cstdio>
#include <vector>

#define ll long long
#include<bits/stdc++.h>

using namespace std;
ll mod = 1e9+7;
ll numberOfPaths(ll xp, ll yp,ll xb,ll yb,ll dp[][2001])
{
    if(xp>xb||yp>yb)
        return 0;
    if(xp==xb&&yp==yb)
        return 1;
   // cout<<dp[xp][-yp]<<" ";
    if(dp[xp][yp]!=-1)
        return dp[xp][yp];
    return dp[xp][yp]=
        (numberOfPaths(xp+1,yp,xb,yb,dp)+numberOfPaths(xp,yp+1,xb,yb,dp))%mod;
}
 

int main() {
    ll xb,yb,xp,yp;
    cin>>xb>>yb>>xp>>yp;
    if(xp!=0&&yp!=0){
     
        xb=xb-xp;
        yb=yb-yp;
           xp=xp-xp;
        yp=yp-yp;
        if(xb<0)
            xb=(-1)*xb;
        if(yb<0)
            yb=(-1)*yb;
    }
    ll dp[2001][2001];
    memset(dp,-1,sizeof(dp));
  //  cout<<xp<<" "<<yp<<" "<<xb<<" "<<yb<<" ";
    ll min_jump=abs(xp-xb)+abs(yp-yb);
    ll max_jump;
    if((xp==yp&&xb==yb)){
        max_jump = 2*min(abs(xp-xb),abs(yp-yb))-1;
    }else{
        max_jump = 2*min(abs(xp-xb),abs(yp-yb));
    }
    if(xp==xb||yb==yp){
        if(xp==yp&&xb==yb)
            cout<<min_jump<<" "<<0<<" "<<0<<" "<<0<<"\n";
        else
        cout<<min_jump<<" "<<1<<" "<<0<<" "<<0<<"\n";
    }else
    cout<<min_jump<<" "<<numberOfPaths(xp,yp,xb,yb,dp)<<" "<<1<<" "<<max_jump<<"\n";

    /* Enter your code here. Read input from STDIN. Print output to STDOUT */   
    return 0;
}

#include <cstdio>
#include <vector>
#include <iostream>
#include <algorithm>
#include <climits>
using namespace std;


int main() {
    int n, m, q;
    cin >> n >> m;
    
    int g[n+1][n+1];
    
    for (int i = 0; i <= n; i++) {
        for (int j = 0; j <= n; j++) {
            if (i == j) g[i][j] = 0;
            else g[i][j] = INT_MAX;
        }
    }
    
    for (int i = 0; i < m; i++) {
        int u, v, w;
        cin >> u >> v >> w;
        
        g[u][v] = w;
    }
    
//     for (int i = 1; i <= n; i++) {
//         for (int j = 1; j <= n; j++) {
//             cout << g[i][j] << " ";
//         }
//         cout << "\n";
//     }
    
    int d0[n+1][n+1];
    for (int i = 1; i <= n; i++) {
        for (int j = 1; j <= n; j++) {
           d0[i][j] = g[i][j];   
        }
    }
    
    for (int k = 1; k <= n; k++) {
        for (int i = 1; i <= n; i++) {
            for (int j = 1; j <= n; j++) {
                if (g[i][k] != INT_MAX && g[k][j] != INT_MAX) {
                    g[i][j] = min(g[i][j], g[i][k] + g[k][j]);
                }
            }
        }
        
        // for (int i = 1; i <= n; i++) {
        //     for (int j = 1; j <= n; j++) {
        //         d0[i][j] = d[i][j];
        //     }
        // }
    }
    
    
    cin >> q;
    while (q--) {
        int a, b;
        cin >> a >> b;
        
        if (a == b) {
            cout << 0 << endl;
        } else if (g[a][b] == INT_MAX) {
            cout << -1 << endl;
        } else {
            cout << g[a][b] << endl;   
        }
    }
    
    return 0;
}

29/12/22, 22:23 - Aditya Shrivastava Bits: #include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

int main() {  
      int t;
      cin>>t;
      while(t--) {
          int n,m;
          cin>>n>>m;
          vector<pair<int,int>>v[n+1];
          for(int i=0;i<m;i++) {  
              int x,y,z;
              cin>>x>>y>>z;
              v[x].push_back({y,z});
              v[y].push_back({x,z});
          }
        
          int s;
          cin>>s;
           
          vector<int>distance(n+1,INT_MAX);  
          vector<int> ans;
          priority_queue< pair<int,int>,vector<pair<int,int>>,greater<pair<int,int>>>pq;
        
          distance[s]=0;
          pq.push({0,s});
          
          int count=0;
          while(!pq.empty()) {
              auto x=pq.top();
              pq.pop();
              if(x.first>distance[x.second]) continue;
              
              for(auto l:v[x.second]) {
                  if(distance[l.first]>distance[x.second]+l.second) {
                      distance[l.first]=distance[x.second]+l.second;
                      pq.push({distance[x.second]+l.second,l.first});
                  }
              }  
          }
   
          for(int i=1;i<=n;i++) {
              if(i==s) continue;
              if(distance[i]==INT_MAX) ans.push_back(-1);
              else ans.push_back(distance[i]);
          }
          
          int max = ans[0];
          for(int i=0;i<ans.size();i++) {
              if(ans[i]>max) max = ans[i];      
          }
          
          cout<<max<<"\n";
      }
    
    return 0;
}

29/12/22, 22:23 - Aditya Shrivastava Bits: #include <cmath>
#include <cstdio>
#include <cstring>
#include <vector>
#include <iostream>
#include <algorithm>
using namespace std;


int solve(vector<vector<int>> &m, vector<vector<bool>> &vis, int i, int j, int n) {
    if (i == n-1 && j == n-1) {
        return 1;
    }
    
    vis[i][j] = 1;
    
    int x1 = 0, x2 = 0, x3 = 0, x4 = 0;
    
    if (j+1 <= n-1 && m[i][j+1] == 1 && !vis[i][j+1]) {
        x1 = solve(m, vis, i, j+1, n);
    }
    
    if (j-1 >= 0 && m[i][j-1] == 1 && !vis[i][j-1]) {
        x2 = solve(m, vis, i, j-1, n);
    }
    
    if (i-1 >= 0 && m[i-1][j] == 1 && !vis[i-1][j]) {
        x3 = solve(m, vis, i-1, j, n);
    }
    
    if (i+1 <= n-1 && m[i+1][j] == 1 && !vis[i+1][j]) {
        x4 = solve(m, vis, i+1, j, n);
    }
    
    vis[i][j] = 0;
    
    return x1+x2+x3+x4;
}


int main() {
    int n;
    cin >> n;
    
    vector<vector<int>> m(n, vector<int> (n));
    
    for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        for (int j = 0; j < n; j++) {
            cin >> m[i][j];
        }
    }
    
    // for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
    //     for (int j = 0; j < n; j++) {
    //         cout << m[i][j] << " ";
    //     }
    //     cout << "\n";
    // }
    
    vector<vector<bool>> vis(n, vector<bool> (n, 0));
    
    // for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
    //     for (int j = 0; j < n; j++) {
    //         cout << vis[i][j] << " ";
    //     }
    //     cout << "\n";
    // }
    
    int res = solve(m, vis, 0, 0, n);
    
    if (res == 0) {
        cout << -1 << endl;
    } else {
        cout << res << endl;
    }

    return 0;
}

31/12/22, 00:53 - GauraV: #include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;
void fastscan(long &number)
{
    //variable to indicate sign of input number
    bool negative = false;
    register long c;
  
    number = 0;
  
    // extract current character from buffer
    c = getchar();
    if (c=='-')
    {
        // number is negative
        negative = true;
  
        // extract the next character from the buffer
        c = getchar();
    }
  
    // Keep on extracting characters if they are integers
    // i.e ASCII Value lies from '0'(48) to '9' (57)
    for (; (c>47 && c<58); c=getchar())
        number = number *10 + c - 48;
  
    // if scanned input has a negative sign, negate the
    // value of the input number
    if (negative)
        number *= -1;
}

     

int main(){
    
    ios_base::sync_with_stdio(false);
    cin.tie(NULL);
    
    long t; fastscan(t);
    for(long i=0 ; i<t ; i++){
      long S;  
    long V, E;  
    fastscan (V);
    fastscan(E);
    vector<vector<long>> adj[V+1];
    
    for(long i=0 ; i<E ; i++){
        long x, y, z; fastscan(x); fastscan(y); fastscan(z);
        vector<long> temp1, temp2;
        temp1.push_back(y);
        temp1.push_back(z);
        temp2.push_back(x);
        temp2.push_back(z);
        adj[x].push_back(temp1);
        adj[y].push_back(temp2);
        
    }
    fastscan(S);

priority_queue<pair<long,long>,vector<pair<long,long>>,greater<pair<long,long>> >pq;
        pq.push({0,S});
        vector<long> distance(V+1);
        for(long i=0 ; i<=V ; i++){
            distance[i] = INT_MAX;
        }
        distance[S] = 0;
        while(!pq.empty()){
            long dis = pq.top().first;
            long node = pq.top().second;
            pq.pop();
            
            for(auto it: adj[node]){
                long edgeweight = it[1];
                long adjnode = it[0];
                if(dis + edgeweight < distance[adjnode]){
                    distance[adjnode] = dis + edgeweight;
                    pq.push({distance[adjnode],adjnode});
                }
            }
        }
        vector<long> ans;
        
         for(int i=1;i<=V;i++) {
              if(i==S) continue;
              if(distance[i]==INT_MAX) continue;
              else ans.push_back(distance[i]);
          }
    long maxi = 0;
    for(long i=0 ; i<ans.size() ; i++){
        maxi = max(maxi, ans[i]);
    }
    cout << maxi << endl;
    }
}

21/07/23, 21:05 - GauraV: #include<bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

static bool comp(pair<long,long> &a, pair<long,long>&b){
    if(a.first == b.first){
        return a.second < b.second;
    }
    return a.first < b.first;
}
int main() {
    double n ; cin >> n;
    vector<pair<long,long>> process;
    for(long i=0 ; i<n ; i++){
        long a,b;
        cin >> a >> b;
        process.push_back({a,b});
    }
    sort(process.begin(), process.end(),comp);
    priority_queue<pair<long,long>, vector<pair<long,long>>, greater<pair<long,long>> > pq;
    long idx=0;
    long currentTime=0;
    long turnaroundtime=0;
    while(!pq.empty() || idx<n){
        if (pq.empty()) {
            currentTime = max(currentTime, process[idx].first);
        }
        while (idx < n && process[idx].first <= currentTime) {
            pq.push({process[idx].second, process[idx].first});
            idx++;
        }
        long arrivaltime = pq.top().second;
        currentTime = currentTime + pq.top().first;
        turnaroundtime = turnaroundtime + currentTime-arrivaltime;
        pq.pop();
    }
    cout << floor(turnaroundtime/n);
    return 0;
}

23/09/23, 20:07 - Aditya Shrivastava Bits: #include <stdio.h>
#include <pthread.h>
#include <malloc.h>
#include <limits.h>

struct Array_3D {
    int h, r, c;
};

void *allocate_memory(void* args) {
    struct Array_3D *dimensions = (struct Array_3D *)args;
    int h = dimensions->h;
    int r = dimensions->r;
    int c = dimensions->c;

    int ***matrix = (int ***)malloc(h * sizeof(int **));

    for (int i = 0; i < h; i++) {
        matrix[i] = (int **)malloc(r * sizeof(int *));
        for (int j = 0; j < r; j++) {
            matrix[i][j] = (int *)malloc(c * sizeof(int));
        }
    }

    pthread_exit((void *)matrix);
}

void take_input(int ***arr, int h, int r, int c) {
    printf("Enter %d 3D matrices of size %dx%d:\n", h, r, c);

    for (int i = 0; i < h; i++) {
        printf("Matrix %d:\n", i + 1);
        for (int j = 0; j < r; j++) {
            printf("Row %d: ", j + 1);
            for (int k = 0; k < c; k++) {
                scanf("%d", &arr[i][j][k]);
            }
        }
    }
}

int Get_row_count(int **matrix, int rows, int cols) {
    int maxOnes = 0;
    int maxRow = -1;

    for (int i = 0; i < rows; i++) {
        int onesCount = 0;
        for (int j = 0; j < cols; j++) {
            if (matrix[i][j] == 1) {
                onesCount++;
            }
        }

        if (onesCount > maxOnes || (onesCount == maxOnes && i < maxRow)) {
            maxOnes = onesCount;
            maxRow = i;
        }
    }

    return maxRow;
}

void *Get_all_Rows(void *arg) {
    int ***arr = (int ***)arg;
    struct Array_3D *dimensions = (struct Array_3D *)arg;
    int h = dimensions->h;
    int r = dimensions->r;
    int c = dimensions->c;

    int *maxRows = (int *)malloc(h * sizeof(int));

    for (int i = 0; i < h; i++) {
        maxRows[i] = -1; // Initialize with -1 in case there are no 1's

        for (int j = 0; j < r; j++) {
            int rowWithMostOnes = Get_row_count(arr[i][j], r, c);
            if (rowWithMostOnes != -1) {
                if (maxRows[i] == -1 || rowWithMostOnes < maxRows[i]) {
                    maxRows[i] = rowWithMostOnes;
                }
            }
        }
    }

    pthread_exit((void *)maxRows);
}

int main() {
    struct Array_3D obj;
    scanf("%d%d%d", &obj.h, &obj.r, &obj.c);
    int i;
    pthread_t thread;

    pthread_create(&thread, NULL, allocate_memory, (void *)&obj);
    int ***arr = NULL;
    pthread_join(thread, (void *)&arr);
    take_input(arr, obj.h, obj.r, obj.c);

    pthread_create(&thread, NULL, Get_all_Rows, (void *)arr);
    int *all_rows = NULL;
    pthread_join(thread, (void *)&all_rows);

    for (i = 0; i < obj.h; i++) {
        printf("%d ", all_rows[i]);
    }
    return 0;
}

25/09/23, 18:47 - Aditya Shrivastava Bits: #include <iostream>
#include <queue>
using namespace std;

struct TreeNode {
    int data;
    TreeNode* left;
    TreeNode* right;
    TreeNode(int val) : data(val), left(nullptr), right(nullptr) {}
};

int minimumJumps(TreeNode* root, int n1, int n2) {
    if (root == nullptr) {
        return -1; // If the tree is empty, return -1
    }

    if (n1 == n2) {
        return 0; // If n1 and n2 are the same, no jumps are needed (distance is 0)
    }

    queue<TreeNode*> q;
    q.push(root);
    int jumps = 0;
    bool n1_found = false, n2_found = false;

    while (!q.empty()) {
        int size = q.size();
        
        for (int i = 0; i < size; i++) {
            TreeNode* node = q.front();
            q.pop();

            if (node->data == n1) {
                n1_found = true;
            }
            
            if (node->data == n2) {
                n2_found = true;
            }

            // Add child nodes to the queue
            if (node->left) {
                q.push(node->left);
            }
            if (node->right) {
                q.push(node->right);
            }
        }

        jumps++; // Increment the number of jumps after processing each level

        if (n1_found && n2_found) {
            return jumps - 1; // Subtract 1 to account for the initial level
        }
    }

    return -1; // Return -1 if n1 or n2 is not found in the tree
}

int main() {
    // Construct a sample binary tree
    TreeNode* root = new TreeNode(1);
    root->left = new TreeNode(2);
    root->right = new TreeNode(3);
    root->left->left = new TreeNode(4);
    root->left->right = new TreeNode(5);
    root->right->left = new TreeNode(6);
    root->right->right = new TreeNode(7);

    int n1, n2;
    cout << "Enter the values of n1 and n2: ";
    cin >> n1 >> n2;

    int result = minimumJumps(root, n1, n2);
    
    if (result != -1) {
        cout << "Minimum jumps from " << n1 << " to " << n2 << " is " << result << endl;
    } else {
        cout << "One or both nodes are not present in the tree or n1 is equal to n2." << endl;
    }

    // Clean up memory (optional)
    delete root->right->right;
    delete root->right->left;
    delete root->right;
    delete root->left->right;
    delete root->left->left;
    delete root->left;
    delete root;

    return 0;
}

25/09/23, 18:50 - Aditya Shrivastava Bits: #include <iostream>
#include <vector>
#include <algorithm>
using namespace std;

int dx[] = {1, -1, 0, 0, 1, -1, 1, -1};
int dy[] = {0, 0, 1, -1, 1, -1, -1, 1};

bool isValid(int x, int y, int m, int n) {
    return x >= 0 && x < m && y >= 0 && y < n;
}

int dfs(char **matrix, int m, int n, char ch, int x, int y) {
    int maxPath = 0;

    for (int dir = 0; dir < 8; dir++) {
        int newX = x + dx[dir];
        int newY = y + dy[dir];

        if (isValid(newX, newY, m, n) && matrix[newX][newY] == ch + 1) {
            int length = 1 + dfs(matrix, m, n, ch + 1, newX, newY);
            maxPath = max(maxPath, length);
        }
    }

    return maxPath;
}

int countConsecutivePaths(char **matrix, int m, int n, char ch) {
    int maxCount = 0;

    for (int i = 0; i < m; i++) {
        for (int j = 0; j < n; j++) {
            if (matrix[i][j] == ch) {
                int length = 1 + dfs(matrix, m, n, ch, i, j);
                maxCount = max(maxCount, length);
            }
        }
    }

    return maxCount;
}

int main() {
    int m, n;
    cout << "Enter the number of rows and columns: ";
    cin >> m >> n;

    char **matrix = new char *[m];
    for (int i = 0; i < m; i++) {
        matrix[i] = new char[n];
        for (int j = 0; j < n; j++) {
            cin >> matrix[i][j];
        }
    }

    char ch;
    cout << "Enter the character to start from: ";
    cin >> ch;

    int result = countConsecutivePaths(matrix, m, n, ch);

    cout << "The longest consecutive path starting from '" << ch << "' has length: " << result << endl;

    // Deallocate memory
    for (int i = 0; i < m; i++) {
        delete[] matrix[i];
    }
    delete[] matrix;

    return 0;
}

05/11/23, 13:08 - GauraV: #include <iostream>
#include <vector>
#include <algorithm>
using namespace std;

int calculateChecksum(int num)
{
  vector<int> digits;
  while (num > 0)
  {
    digits.push_back(num % 10);
    num /= 10;
  }
  if (digits.empty())
  {
    return 0;
  }
  auto minMax = minmax_element(digits.begin(), digits.end());
  int sum = 0;
  for (int digit : digits)
  {
    if (digit != *minMax.first && digit != *minMax.second)
    {
      sum += digit;
    }
  }
  return sum;
}

int main()
{
  int N;
  cin >> N;

  vector<int> numbers(N);
  for (int i = 0; i < N; ++i)
  {
    cin >> numbers[i];
  }

  int totalChecksum = 0;
  for (int num : numbers)
  {
    totalChecksum += calculateChecksum(num);
  }

  cout << totalChecksum << endl;

  return 0;
}

01/12/23, 20:05 - Aditya Shrivastava Bits: bool canDistributeEquallyHelper(const vector<int> &coins, vector<int> &currentSums, int targetSum, int index)
{
  // Base case: check if all children received the target sum
  if (index == coins.size())
  {
    return currentSums[0] == targetSum && currentSums[1] == targetSum && currentSums[2] == targetSum;
  }

  // Try distributing the current coin to each child
  for (int i = 0; i < 3; ++i)
  {
    if (currentSums[i] + coins[index] <= targetSum)
    {
      currentSums[i] += coins[index];
      if (canDistributeEquallyHelper(coins, currentSums, targetSum, index + 1))
      {
        return true;
      }
      currentSums[i] -= coins[index]; // Backtrack
    }
  }

  return false;
}

bool coinTrouble(const vector<int> &coins)
{
  // Calculate the total sum of coins
  int totalSum = 0;
  for (int coin : coins)
  {
    totalSum += coin;
  }

  // Check if the total sum is divisible by 3
  if (totalSum % 3 != 0)
  {
    return false;
  }

  // Calculate the target sum for each child
  int targetSum = totalSum / 3;

  // Vector to store the current sum for each child
  vector<int> currentSums(3, 0);

  // Check if the coins can be distributed equally
  return canDistributeEquallyHelper(coins, currentSums, targetSum, 0);
}

01/12/23, 20:19 - Aditya Shrivastava Bits: int makeStringSteady(string &input)
{
  unordered_map<char, int> letterCount;
  for (char ch : input)
  {
    letterCount[ch]++;
  }

  int targetCount = input.length() / 4;
  int left = 0, right = 0;
  int minLength = INT_MAX;

  while (right < input.length())
  {
    letterCount[input[right]]--;

    while (letterCount['B'] <= targetCount && letterCount['D'] <= targetCount &&
           letterCount['U'] <= targetCount && letterCount['H'] <= targetCount)
    {

      minLength = min(minLength, right - left + 1);

      letterCount[input[left]]++;
      left++;
    }

    right++;
  }

  return minLength;
}
